Method: 设计了一个结合零样本自然语言推理（Zero-shot NLI）与时间聚合的结构化流程，专门建模了新闻的时效性和事件依赖的影响期。此外，引入了一个多层级可解释性框架，能够将预测结果追溯至词元（token）和文章层面，并生成基于证据的自然语言解释。

Result: 实验表明，零样本方法在预测表现上始终未能超越简单的基准模型，特别是在预测负向价格波动时表现尤为疲软。然而，该模型提供的可解释性信号能够有效区分预测结果的可信度，从而在预测准确性有限的情况下依然具备实际应用价值。

Conclusion: 零样本金融NLP在短期股价预测方面存在明显的结构性局限，难以通过简单的文本情感映射实现盈利。未来的研究应从追求预测准确度转向构建强调可解释性、透明度和不确定性感知的主动决策支持系统。

Abstract: Can financial news reliably predict short-term stock movements? Despite advances in large language models, this question remains unresolved. We revisit this problem using a zero-shot natural language processing framework, investigating whether models can extract actionable signals from financial news without domain-specific training. We design a structured pipeline that combines zero-shot natural language inference with temporal aggregation, explicitly modelling recency and event-dependent impact horizons when integrating information across articles. To address the need for transparency in high-stakes settings, we introduce a multi-layered explainability framework that links predictions to token-level, article-level, and aggregate evidence, and produces grounded natural language rationales. Across multiple models and prediction horizons, we find that zero-shot approaches consistently fail to outperform simple baselines, with particularly weak performance on negative movements, suggesting deeper structural limitations in mapping news sentiment to short-term price dynamics. However, explainability signals reliably distinguish between trustworthy and unreliable predictions, offering practical value even when accuracy is limited. These findings highlight the limits of zero-shot financial NLP and motivate a shift toward decision-support systems that prioritise transparency and uncertainty awareness. Code: https://github.com/alimert05/zero-shot-stock-xai

### [78] [On The Effectiveness-Fluency Trade-Off In LLM Conditioning: A Systematic Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12234)
*Iuri Macocco,Pau Rodríguez,Arno Blaas,Luca Zappella,Marco Baroni,Xavier Suau*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文系统分析了大型语言模型的概念控制方法，发现高效的引导手段常以损害流畅度为代价，且指令微调会削弱激活引导的有效性；同时证明了简单文本指标可作为评估控制效果的经济替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对大语言模型在可靠部署中面临的控制难题，现有的评估方式往往忽视了模型输出的生成质量，缺乏对不同控制方法及其权衡关系的系统性理解，因此需要深入探究各种方法在不同场景下的表现及局限性。

Method: 研究者系统地评估了多种条件控制方法（包括激活引导、提示工程和监督微调），涵盖了概念注入和概念移除两种场景。通过对比不同方法在基础模型和指令微调模型上的表现，并结合廉价文本指标与LLM-as-judge评分的相关性分析，系统地量化了性能折中。

Result: 1. 高效的引导方法往往以牺牲模型输出的流畅度为代价；2. 激活引导方法在指令微调模型上的有效性远低于基础模型；3. 提示工程和监督微调在概念注入方面表现良好，但在概念移除方面效果欠佳；4. 廉价的文本指标能有效替代昂贵的LLM-as-judge评分，并能揭示控制方法的行为特征。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了大型语言模型（LLM）控制方法在效果与生成质量之间的权衡，指出了指令微调对激活引导方法的显著抑制作用，并验证了廉价文本指标作为评估工具的有效性，为后续更可靠的模型部署提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Controlling the output of Large Language Models (LLMs) is a central challenge for their reliable deployment, yet a clear understanding of the involved trade-offs remains elusive. Current approaches to conditioning are often evaluated with a narrow focus on their effectiveness at injecting or removing a target concept, neglecting generation quality. We systematically investigate a range of conditioning methods in both injection and removal scenarios. We find that efficient steering methods frequently achieve conditioning at a steep cost to fluency. Furthermore, we identify a critical yet previously overlooked interaction with the training paradigm: activation steering methods are far less effective on instruction-tuned models than on their base counterparts. Simple prompting and full-fledged supervised fine-tuning, on the other hand, are viable options for concept injection, but are not as good at concept removal. Finally, cheaply computed textual metrics highly correlate to costly LLM-as-judge scores, and provide insights on the behavior of conditioning methods.

### [79] [VIA-SD: Verification via Intra-Model Routing for Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12243)
*Yuchen Xian,Yang He,Yunqiu Xu,Yi Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: VIA-SD 提出了一种多层级推测解码框架，通过在草稿模型和完整验证模型之间加入一个基于模型内路由的“精简验证器”，有效处理中等难度令牌，从而显著提升了 LLM 的推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推测解码（SD）多采用“二元决策”模式（即要么接受，要么由全量大模型重计算）。研究发现，许多被拒绝的令牌其实可以通过轻量级的子模型正确验证，无需动用昂贵的完整大模型，从而造成了计算资源的浪费。因此，作者旨在通过引入一个中间层的“精简验证器”来优化验证流程，降低推理成本。

Method: 提出了 VIA-SD（基于模型内路由的推测解码验证），构建了一个多层级框架：1. 高置信度令牌直接接受；2. 中等置信度令牌由从大型验证模型派生的“精简子模型”进行路由验证和重生成；3. 低置信度令牌交由完整大模型进行验证。该方法利用模型内路由技术，无需修改现有模型的训练过程即可与现有 SD 框架兼容。

Result: 在四个代表性任务和多个模型家族上，VIA-SD 将令牌拒绝率降低了 0.10-0.22，相比传统的强基线 SD 方法提升了 10-20% 的速度，对比非推测解码推理则实现了 2.5-3 倍的加速。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，多层级推测解码（Multi-tier SD）是一个可扩展且高效的 LLM 推理范式。通过在草稿生成和完整模型验证之间引入“精简验证器（Slim-verifier）”，可以显著降低拒绝率，并在不改变现有训练流程的情况下提升整体推理速度。

Abstract: Speculative decoding (SD) addresses the high inference costs of LLMs by having lightweight drafters generate candidates for large verifiers to validate in parallel. Existing draft-verify methods use binary decisions: accept or fully recompute. Yet we find that many rejected tokens can be verified correctly by a slim submodel derived from the full verifier via intra-model routing, instead of the full verifier. This motivates our slim-verifier to handle tokens requiring moderate verification resources, reducing expensive large-model calls. We propose Verification via Intra-Model Routing for Speculative Decoding (VIA-SD), a multi-tier framework using a routed slim-verifier. Draft tokens are processed hierarchically: direct acceptance for high-confidence cases, slim-verifier regeneration for medium-confidence cases, and full-model verification for uncertain cases. Across four representative tasks and multiple model families, VIA-SD reduces rejection rates by 0.10-0.22 and delivers 10-20% speedups over strong SD baselines, while achieving 2.5-3x acceleration over non-drafting decoding. Moreover, VIA-SD is compatible with existing SD frameworks without modifying their training procedures. Our results suggest multi-tier SD as a general paradigm for scalable and efficient LLM inference. Project page: https://zju-xyc.github.io/VIA-SD-Project-Page/

</details>

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) in medicine are mainly evaluated using multiple-choice question answering (MCQA), which can overestimate real clinical ability due to guessing strategies and answer biases. To address these limitations, we introduce an expanded and more challenging benchmark based on Polish medical exams, adding over 15,000 questions, two new domains, and four structural modifications that reduce MCQA-specific artifacts and better test reasoning. We evaluate 21 LLMs and show that evaluation design strongly affects results. Under our harder setup, the best model (Qwen3.5-122B) drops by 28.4 and 31 pp on English and Polish exams, respectively. Despite low evidence of data contamination, standard MCQA scores do not reliably reflect true medical competence. To facilitate further research, we make our benchmark publicly available.

### [81] [Beyond Fully Random Masking: Attention-Guided Denoising and Optimization for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12273)
*Jia Deng,Junyi Li,Wayne Xin Zhao,Jinpeng Wang,Hongyu Lu,Ji-Rong Wen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种注意力引导的扩散大语言模型（dLLM）优化框架AGDO，通过将去噪顺序和训练重点与注意力机制中的token依赖性对齐，有效提升了模型在推理任务中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散大语言模型（dLLM）后训练方法多采用随机掩码策略，未能充分考虑token之间内在的依赖关系，限制了模型在推理任务中的表现。因此，需要一种能够利用注意力机制来指导训练和去噪的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为AGDO的注意力引导去噪与优化框架：1. 基于注意力分析，揭示了token依赖性与生成稳定性的关系；2. 根据注意力结构确定去噪顺序；3. 在监督微调（SFT）和强化学习阶段，重点增强对“注意力关键token”的学习和优化。

Result: 在数学和编程基准测试中，AGDO框架在推理能力上均表现优异，持续超越了现有的先进dLLM后训练方法。

Abstract: Diffusion large language models (dLLMs) offer an efficient alternative to autoregressive models through parallel decoding, yet existing post-training methods largely rely on random masking strategies that overlook intrinsic token dependencies. In this work, we present an empirical analysis of attention in dLLMs and show that tokens attending more strongly to unmasked context exhibit greater generation stability and play a critical role in reasoning. Motivated by these findings, we propose AGDO, an attention-guided denoising and optimization framework that aligns both training and optimization with attention-derived dependencies. AGDO determines the denoising order based on attention structure and emphasizes attention-critical tokens during supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning. Experiments on mathematical and coding benchmarks demonstrate that AGDO consistently improves reasoning performance, outperforming state-of-the-art post-training methods for dLLMs.

</details>


### [82] [Measuring Epistemic Resilience of LLMs Under Misleading Medical Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12291)
*Hongjian Zhou,Xinyu Zou,Jinge Wu,Sean Wu,Junchi Yu,Bradley Max Segal,Tobias Erich Niebuhr,Sara Amro,Michael Petrus,Sheikh Momin,Alexandra M. Cardoso Pinto,Rachel Niesen,Laura Sophie Wegner,Dhruv Darji,Jung Moses Koo,Joshua Fieggen,Kapil Narain,Mingde Zeng,Lei Clifton,Linda Shapiro,Fenglin Liu,David A. Clifton*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了医疗大模型在面对误导性上下文时表现出的“认知韧性”不足，即便在考试中表现优异的模型也极易被误导，导致高风险的错误决策，亟需建立新的鲁棒性评估基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前医疗大模型在医学执照考试中表现优异，导致人们误以为高分即代表安全的医学判断。研究者旨在揭示这一假设的脆弱性，即模型极易受到误导性上下文的干扰而放弃原本正确的答案，从而评估模型的“认知韧性”。

Method: 研究团队构建了包含10,932个医疗问题及48,889对误导性语境选项的基准测试集“MedMisBench”。该基准涵盖医疗推理、代理能力及患者旅程评估，旨在通过注入误导性信息观察模型能否保持正确判断，并邀请14位临床专家对模型在误导下的表现进行危害性评估。

Result: 在11种模型配置测试中，面对误导性信息，模型平均准确率从71.1%骤降至38.0%，攻击成功率高达51.5%。其中，权威框架下的虚假信息和例外情况篡改最具破坏力，临床专家评审显示38.2%的模型错误回答具有严重的潜在临床伤害风险。

Conclusion: 现有医疗大语言模型评估体系存在结构性盲点，仅衡量知识储备而忽视了面对误导性信息时的判断稳定性。研究强调，必须将“认知韧性”纳入医疗大模型评估的核心指标，以防止模型在真实临床场景中产生潜在危害。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) now reach expert-level scores on medical licensing exams, encouraging the assumption that high scores imply safe medical judgment while patients increasingly use them for health advice. We show this assumption is fragile: when misleading context is injected into questions that LLMs originally answer correctly, they abandon the correct answer. We call the ability to maintain correct judgment under adversarial context epistemic resilience, and introduce MedMisBench to measure it. MedMisBench contains 10,932 medical question items and 48,889 misleading context-option pairs spanning medical reasoning, agentic capability, and patient-journey evaluation. Across 11 model configurations, mean accuracy falls from 71.1% on original questions to 38.0% under focused misleading context, with 51.5% attack success. The most damaging injections are formal, rule-like fabrications: authority-framed falsehoods reach 69.5% attack success and exception-poisoning claims reach 64.1%. A 14-member clinical panel from 7 countries identified serious potential harm in 38.2% of reviewed cases. MedMisBench exposes a structural blind spot in LLM evaluation in medical settings: existing benchmarks measure what models know, but not whether they preserve correct medical judgment under misleading context.

</details>


### [83] [Measuring Semantic Progress in Multi-turn Dialogue via Information Gain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12332)
*Paul He,Shiva Kasiviswanathan,Dominik Janzing*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于嵌入空间信息论的新度量指标，通过量化多轮对话中的“语义进展”（即信息的有效积累）来评估对话质量，实现了比大模型评判更高效、更具可解释性且与人类判断高度一致的评价效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多轮对话的质量难以仅通过单次回复进行评估，现有的“大模型作为评判者”（LLM-as-a-judge）方法存在计算成本高、不可复现且缺乏可解释性等问题。研究者旨在定义并量化信息检索对话中的核心维度——“语义进展”（即随着对话推进，新颖且相关的有用信息的积累）。

Method: 该研究提出了一个基于信息论的度量标准，将语义进展形式化为“条件于问题的目标不确定性降低”。具体实现上，采用高斯分布公式并利用嵌入空间的对数行列式（log-determinant）结构进行计算，该方法具备单调性、信息增益的可加性以及对冗余信息的边际递减效应等数学性质。

Result: 在MT-Bench、Chatbot Arena和UltraFeedback等数据集上的实验表明，该度量标准与人类评价具有高度的一致性，在部分基准上优于主流的大模型评判方法。此外，该方法支持轻量级嵌入模型，可在仅使用CPU的环境下高效运行。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了“语义进展”可以被形式化为问答过程中的不确定性降低，且基于嵌入空间的对数行列式度量方法是评估多轮对话质量的有效、高效且可解释的替代方案，无需依赖昂贵的大语言模型推理。

Abstract: Evaluating multi-turn dialogue is challenging because quality emerges across turns rather than within individual responses. We focus on a key dimension of information-seeking dialogue: semantic progress, defined as the accumulation of new, question-relevant, and non-redundant information over the course of a conversation. We formalize semantic progress as question-conditioned uncertainty reduction and introduce an information-theoretic metric that approximates it in embedding space. Our main estimator uses a tractable Gaussian formulation with closed-form updates, while a complementary maximum-entropy argument shows why log-determinant structure arises more broadly when only second-order embedding information is retained. This formulation yields desirable theoretical properties, including monotonicity, additive decomposition of total information gain across turns, and diminishing returns for redundant evidence. Unlike LLM-as-a-judge approaches, our metric requires no autoregressive inference at evaluation time and is fully reproducible for a fixed embedding model. Experiments on MT-Bench, Chatbot Arena, and UltraFeedback show that the proposed metric achieves competitive agreement with human judgments despite targeting only semantic progress, with improved alignment on MT-Bench and UltraFeedback compared to several LLM-based judges. Notably, the method remains effective with lightweight embedding models under CPU-only execution, indicating that semantic progress can be captured without reliance on large model capacity.

</details>


### [84] [ALIGNBEAM : Inference-Time Alignment Transfer via Cross-Vocabulary Logit Mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12342)
*Chirag Chawla,Pratinav Seth,Vinay Kumar Sankarapu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了解决领域微调导致的大模型安全性下降问题，本文提出了 ALIGNBEAM。它通过在推理时将安全锚点模型的知识迁移至目标模型（支持异构词表），并利用轻量级裁判筛选安全输出，在无需重新训练的前提下显著增强了模型的安全防御能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在进行特定领域微调后，虽然提升了专业能力，但往往会牺牲安全性，导致模型更容易响应恶意提示。现有的基于逻辑混合（logit-mixing）的推理时防御手段限制了必须共享词表，无法在异构模型家族间应用，因此需要一种更通用的安全防御方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ALIGNBEAM 的推理时防御方法。该方法通过在解码的每一步，将安全锚点模型的 Logits 逐标记翻译（mapping）至目标模型的词表空间，从而解除对词表共享的限制；随后，利用一个小型 LLM 判别器从 K 个候选生成结果中选择最安全的一个。该方法无需修改模型权重。

Result: 在跨词表和同词表评估场景下，ALIGNBEAM 显著提升了模型在对抗性基准测试中的拒绝率，同时保持了良好的任务准确度，并将推理开销控制在实际可接受的范围内。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了安全对齐可以在推理阶段跨模型家族进行迁移，无需修改任何模型的权重。ALIGNBEAM 提供了一种灵活、高效且无需训练的防御机制，能够有效应对领域微调带来的安全降级问题，同时兼顾了任务性能与推理成本。

Abstract: Domain fine-tuning degrades the safety of large language models: fine-tuned specialists readily comply with harmful prompts framed in domain language. Existing inference-time defenses that mix logits from a safe anchor model require both models to share a vocabulary, which rules them out for the cross-family specialists where safety is most degraded. We present ALIGNBEAM, a training-free method that lifts this restriction by translating anchor logits into the target model's vocabulary token-by-token at each decoding step; a small LLM judge then selects the safest among K candidate continuations. No weights are changed, and the safety-utility trade-off can be tuned at deployment without retraining. Across both cross-vocabulary and same-vocabulary evaluation pairs, ALIGNBEAM substantially raises refusal on adversarial benchmarks while keeping task accuracy and inference overhead within practical bounds. The results show that safety alignment can be transferred between model families at inference time, without touching either model's weights.

</details>


### [85] [Verifiable Environments Are LEGO Bricks: Recursive Composition for Reasoning Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12373)
*Hao Xiang,Qiaoyu Tang,Le Yu,Yaojie Lu,Xianpei Han,Ben He,Le Sun,Bowen Yu,Peng Wang,Hongyu Lin,Dayiheng Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RACES 是一个通过递归组合基础验证环境来自动生成复杂训练任务的框架，有效解决了大语言模型强化学习中环境构建的线性瓶颈，显著增强了模型的推理泛化能力并提升了环境利用效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型强化学习依赖人工构建环境，受限于线性扩展瓶颈，难以实现大规模的推理能力泛化。研究旨在解决如何高效、可扩展地构建多样化可验证环境的问题。

Method: 提出 RACES（递归自动化环境组合）框架，将可验证环境视为可组合的构建块。通过定义序列（SEQUENTIAL）、并行（PARALLEL）、排序（SORT）和选择（SELECT）等算子，基于“输出类型匹配输入类型”的逻辑，自动将基础环境融合成更复杂的新环境，从而实现环境规模的指数级扩展。

Result: RACES 在 DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B 和 Qwen3-14B 模型上表现优异，在六个未见过的基准测试中平均分提升了 2.3 至 3.1 分；同时，仅需 50 个基础环境即可达到 300 个独立环境的训练效果，显著提升了资源利用效率。

Conclusion: RACES 提供了一种通过递归组合已验证环境来突破强化学习数据规模限制的有效途径，不仅显著提升了大语言模型的推理泛化能力，还极大提高了环境构建和利用的效率。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) with verifiable environments has emerged as a powerful approach for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). While prior research demonstrates that scaling environment quantity improves RL performance, existing manual or individual construction methods suffer from linear scaling limits, thereby hindering scalable reasoning generalization. This paper introduces RACES (\textbf{R}ecursive \textbf{A}utomated \textbf{C}omposition for \textbf{E}nvironment \textbf{S}caling), a framework that conceptualizes verifiable environments as composable building blocks that can be recursively assembled. The key insight is that when the codomain (output type) of one environment matches the domain (input type) of another, they can be automatically fused into a new verifiable environment, enabling recursive composition. RACES is implemented with 300 individual environments and defines a set of composition operators (\textsc{SEQUENTIAL}, \textsc{PARALLEL}, \textsc{SORT}, and \textsc{SELECT}) that induce diverse reasoning patterns. Extensive experiments show that RL training on these composite environments consistently enhances reasoning generalization. Specifically, RACES improves DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B by an average of 3.1 points (from 48.2 to 51.3) and boosts Qwen3-14B performance from 58.8 to 61.1 on six benchmarks, which are unseen during the construction of training environments. Moreover, RACES achieves performance comparable to training on 300 individual environments using only 50 base environments, demonstrating significant efficiency in environment utilization.

</details>


### [86] [Which Models Are Our Models Built On? Auditing Invisible Dependencies in Modern LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12385)
*Sanjay Adhikesaven,Haoxiang Sun,Sewon Min*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ModSleuth 是一款旨在揭示大模型复杂依赖关系的代理系统，通过自动追踪公共工件构建依赖图，成功识别了模型生态中的多重合规风险与技术文档不一致问题，为大模型的透明度建设提供了重要工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代大模型训练流水线中存在极其复杂的递归依赖，且相关信息散落在不同的公共工件中，人类难以手动追踪。这种碎片化导致了透明度缺失，使得模型开发者和用户难以识别潜在的法律、技术及合规风险。

Method: 开发了 ModSleuth 代理系统，通过定义直接与间接依赖关系，建立以操作为中心的异构依赖图模型，并采用跨名称、版本和存储库的实体解析技术，实现对 LLM 依赖关系的递归重构与来源溯源。

Result: 通过对四个具有丰富公共工件的 LLM 发布版进行分析，ModSleuth 成功恢复了 1,060 个来源验证的依赖项，构建了大规模依赖图。研究发现，这些图谱揭示了多跳许可证义务、训练-评估耦合、以及发布与训练工件之间的不一致性等关键问题。

Conclusion: ModSleuth 揭示了现代大模型开发中极其复杂且碎片化的依赖关系，强调了构建透明度工具对于理解模型生态系统的重要性。该系统通过自动化和规范化的方式，能够有效识别潜在的法律合规风险（如许可证义务）和技术风险（如训练数据泄露与版本不一致）。

Abstract: Modern LLM training pipelines increasingly rely on other models to generate data, filter corpora, judge outputs, and guide development decisions. These dependencies are recursive: a model may depend on an upstream artifact whose own dependencies are documented only in separate releases and artifacts. As a result, the full dependency structure is fragmented across heterogeneous public artifacts, with complexity and recursive depth far outpacing humans' ability to trace. We introduce ModSleuth, an agentic system that recursively reconstructs LLM dependency graphs from public artifacts with source-grounded evidence. We find that the primary challenge is no longer information extraction, but defining what constitutes a dependency and reconciling artifact references across inconsistent documentation. We address these challenges through a formalization that distinguishes direct and indirect dependencies, represents heterogeneous pipeline roles through operation-centered relationships, and resolves artifact identities across names, versions, and repositories. Applying ModSleuth to four public-artifact-rich LLM releases, we recover 1,060 source-verified dependencies and construct large-scale dependency graphs of modern LLM development. These graphs reveal multi-hop license obligations, train-evaluation coupling, discrepancies between released and training-time artifacts, and documentation inconsistencies that would otherwise be difficult to uncover. We release ModSleuth and the resulting dependency graphs to support transparent analysis of the increasingly complex ecosystems underlying modern LLMs.

</details>


### [87] [System Report for CCL25-Eval Task 5: New Dataset and LoRA-Fine-Tuned Qwen2.5](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12392)
*Haotao Xie*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对大模型在古诗词理解上的不足，通过构建高质量数据集CCPoetry-49K并采用LoRA微调Qwen2.5模型，显著提升了模型在古诗词翻译与情感分析任务中的专业性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型在古诗词翻译与理解方面多将其视为通用任务，忽视了古诗词特有的艺术与情感表达特征，且缺乏高质量的领域专属数据集，导致模型在该领域的表现受限。

Method: 1. 将古诗词鉴赏拆解为术语解释、语义解读和情感推断三个子任务；2. 对公开数据集进行清洗与对齐，构建了包含约4.9万条高质量指令微调数据（CCPoetry-49K）；3. 基于Qwen2.5-14B模型，采用LoRA（低秩自适应）技术进行领域特定微调，开发出PoetryQwen模型。

Result: 在CCL25-Eval任务5的基准测试中，PoetryQwen的得分为0.757，相较于基线模型Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct（0.690）提升了9.7%，显著增强了模型对古诗词的精确翻译与情感理解能力。

Conclusion: 通过构建高质量专业数据集并结合针对性的微调策略，本研究成功提升了大模型在古诗词精确翻译与情感语义理解方面的表现，为领域特定大模型的优化提供了有效路径。

Abstract: Recently, large language models (LLMs) have achieved promising progress in the fields of classical Chinese translation and the generation of classical poetry. However, domain-specific research on precise translation and affective-semantic understanding of classical poetry remains limited. The main challenge is that most studies treat the poetic appreciation task as a general-domain problem, neglecting the distinctive features of poetic appreciation, while high-quality and domain-specific datasets are extremely limited. To address this limitation, we decompose the task into three subtasks: term interpretation, semantic interpretation, and emotional inference. Based on multiple open-source datasets, we perform data cleansing and alignment to construct the Classical Chinese Poetry Instruction Pair Dataset (CCPoetry-49K), which comprises 49,404 high-quality instruction-response pairs explicitly optimized for this domain. We then propose a domain-specialized LLM, called PoetryQwen, by applying Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) to fine-tune the Qwen2.5-14B model. Experimental results on the CCL25-Eval Task 5 benchmark demonstrate that PoetryQwen achieves a score of 0.757, representing a 9.7% improvement over the Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct baseline (0.690). These findings clearly indicate that PoetryQwen significantly enhances performance in precise translation and emotional understanding of classical poetry. We present new dataset and methodological considerations intended to support the domain-specific optimization of LLMs.

### [88] [Context-Driven Incremental Compression for Multi-Turn Dialogue Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12411)
*Yeongseo Jung,Jaehyeok Kim,Eunseo Jung,Jiachuan Wang,Yongqi Zhang,Ka Chun Cheung,Simon See,Lei Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对长对话中上下文处理效率低下及信息丢失的问题，本文提出了 C-DIC 框架，通过引入可修订的线程化记忆与创新的跨轮训练机制，在降低计算成本的同时保证了长程对话的逻辑连贯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着对话长度增加，现有的基于原始上下文的建模方式会导致计算成本激增。简单的截断或摘要方法会导致信息丢失，而现有的压缩技术缺乏跨轮记忆共享与修订机制，导致误差累积，难以维持长对话的稳健性。

Method: 提出“上下文驱动增量压缩”（C-DIC）框架，将对话视为交织的语境线程，建立可修订的紧凑型对话记忆库。通过“检索-修订-回写”机制实现跨轮信息共享与更新，并采用适配多轮对话的截断反向传播（TBPTT）技术来学习跨轮依赖，避免了全历史反向传播的计算负担。

Result: 在长文本对话基准测试中，C-DIC 表现优异，在数百轮对话中展现出稳定的推理延迟和困惑度（Perplexity），显著提升了对话建模的效率与效果。

Conclusion: C-DIC 通过引入可修订的线程化记忆机制和针对多轮对话优化的训练方法，有效解决了长对话中上下文压缩的效率与信息流失问题，为构建高效、可扩展的长程对话模型提供了一种稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: Modern conversational agents condition on an ever-growing dialogue history at each turn, incurring redundant attention and encoding costs that grow with conversation length. Naive truncation or summarization degrades fidelity, while existing context compressors lack cross-turn memory sharing or revision, causing information loss and compounding errors in long dialogues. We revisit the context compression under conversational dynamics and empirically present its fragility. To improve both efficiency and robustness, we introduce Context-Driven Incremental Compression (C-DIC), which treats a conversation as interleaved contextual threads and stores revisable per-thread compression states in a single, compact dialogue memory. At each turn, a lightweight retrieve, revise, and write-back loop shares information across turns and updates stale memories, stabilizing long-horizon behavior. In addition, we adapt truncated backpropagation-through-time (TBPTT) to our multi-turn setting, learning cross-turn dependencies without full-history backpropagation. Extensive experiments on long-form dialogue benchmarks demonstrate superior performance and efficiency of C-DIC; notably, C-DIC shows stable inference latency and perplexity over hundreds of dialogue turns, supporting a scalable path to high-quality dialogue modeling.

</details>

### [89] [Restless bandits with imperfect binary feedback: PCL-indexability analysis and computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11192)
*José Niño-Mora*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于PCL的分析框架，用于解决具有不完美反馈的二元状态不安分强盗问题，并通过解析推导与高效数值计算，验证了MP索引策略的卓越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对机会频谱接入中存在的传感误差问题，研究具有二元潜在状态和不完美反馈的不安分强盗问题，旨在解决传统方法在验证索引性与计算Whittle索引方面的局限性。

Method: 利用基于部分守恒定律（PCL）的分析框架，结合确定性骨架、更新分解（renewal decompositions）和字组合学（combinatorics on words）方法，推导折扣奖励与资源度量，并开发了高效的数值方案来计算MP索引。

Result: 实现了在多种阈值机制下的解析表达，完成了PCL索引性条件的验证；在其余机制下，通过数值实验验证了MP索引的有效性，并证明其性能显著优于传统基准策略。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个高效的分析与计算框架，能够验证不安分强盗问题（Restless Bandits）的索引性，并通过数值实验证明了其提出的MP索引策略优于现有的基准策略。

Abstract: We study restless bandits with binary latent states and imperfect binary feedback, motivated by opportunistic spectrum access with sensing errors. For the associated belief-state model, we develop a partial conservation laws (PCL)-based analytical and computational framework for establishing indexability and evaluating the Whittle index, building on a verification theorem for real-state discounted restless bandits. The framework analyzes the stochastic dynamics via an associated deterministic skeleton, renewal decompositions, and combinatorics on words. It yields tractable expressions for discounted reward and resource metrics in several threshold regimes, enabling full verification of the PCL-indexability conditions there. For the remaining regime, where a complete analytic verification is not achieved in this paper, we derive efficient numerical schemes for computing the relevant marginal metrics and the marginal productivity (MP) index, which equals the Whittle index when those conditions hold. Extensive computational experiments provide strong evidence that these conditions also hold in that regime across broad parameter ranges and without the stringent parameter restrictions imposed in prior work. The experiments further show that theMP index policy typically outperforms standard benchmark policies, often by a substantial margin.

### [90] [To Intervene or Not: Guiding Inference-time Alignment with Probabilistic Model Blending](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11201)
*Jin Gan,Xin Li,Jun Luo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对推理时大模型对齐中引导可靠性参差不齐的问题，BlendIn 框架引入了质量感知加权机制，通过动态融合多模型知识，显著提升了对齐的有效性与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理时对齐方法往往不加评估地采纳特定已对齐模型的引导，而作者的研究发现这些引导的有效性在不同模型间差异极大。无效引导不仅无法改善模型输出，反而会导致模型混淆并引发过度干预，从而降低整体性能。

Method: 提出了一种名为 BlendIn 的推理时对齐框架。该方法摒弃了传统的二元决策（是否采纳引导），转而采用质量感知策略，根据模型在不同语境下的可靠性，对不同模型的知识贡献进行动态加权，从而构建出混合概率分布。

Result: 实验结果表明，BlendIn 能够有效保留有益引导并抑制不可靠建议，在具有挑战性的模型对上实现了性能的一致性提升，最高提升幅度达 50%。

Conclusion: BlendIn 提供了一种创新的推理时对齐框架，通过质量感知的比例加权机制，有效解决了传统推理时对齐中盲目采纳引导导致的模型混淆问题，显著提升了对齐效率与性能，为大模型的安全与有效部署提供了有力工具。

Abstract: The wide deployment of LLMs has made model alignment necessary to make newly trained models safely and effectively respond to user instructions. Among different methods, inference-time alignment is often cheaper as it intervenes (i.e., offers guidances) only during output generation. Existing proposals apply guidances extracted from certain aligned models without properly assessing their reliability. Nonetheless, our systematic evaluation reveals that guidance effectiveness varies drastically across models; since ineffective guidances lead to further confusion and thus further interventions, the resulting excessive interventions typically indicate poor performance. To make interventions more effective and thus more efficient, we introduce BlendIn, an inference-time alignment framework that shifts from binary decisions to creating hybrid distributions integrating both models' knowledge. BlendIn stabilizes inference-time alignment by performing quality-aware alignment and proportionally weighting each model's contribution based on reliability. Compared with existing works, it preserves beneficial guidance while downweighting unreliable suggestions. BlendIn provides both diagnostic signals and mitigation strategies for misaligned guidance, achieving consistent and up to 50% performance improvement on challenging model pairs. Our code is available at: https://github.com/DecayingSeart/BlendIn.

### [91] [Dual-Stance Evaluation of Sycophancy: The Structure of Agreement and the Limits of Intervention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11205)
*Matthew James Buchan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现，尽管大模型能几何区分“奉承”与“事实”，但目前的激活转向技术无法在不损害事实表达的前提下抑制奉承，揭示了模型表示空间的可读性与可控性之间存在巨大鸿沟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的激活转向研究通常只关注模型是否能减少奉承行为（sycophancy），而忽略了测试这种干预是否会非预期地抑制模型对事实正确信息的表达。作者旨在探究是否存在某种转向方向，能够区分“迎合用户观点”与“基于事实的共识”。

Method: 作者引入了“双立场评估（dual-stance evaluation）”方法，在 Llama-3-8B-Instruct 模型上测试了“质心差转向（centroid-difference steering）”技术。该方法通过在同一主题的正反两种立场上进行评估，分析模型在减少奉承行为的同时，是否会误伤事实性共识的表达。

Result: 实验发现，尽管模型在几何空间中将奉承性共识与事实性共识表示在不同的子空间内，但现有的转向向量投影在两者上几乎相等。因此，试图减少奉承的转向行为不可避免地会削弱模型对事实正确陈述的认同，表明该干预方法缺乏选择性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了“激活转向”技术在 LLM 可解释性与控制中的局限性：即使模型在几何上能够区分奉承行为与事实性共识，现有的线性转向方法也无法实现选择性干预。这一发现强调了“从激活中可读”并不等同于“通过激活可写”。

Abstract: Activation steering can shift LLM behaviour, but standard evaluations do not typically test whether a sycophancy-reduction direction also suppresses agreement with factually correct statements. We introduce dual-stance evaluation, which tests both stances of each topic, and apply it to centroid-difference steering on Llama-3-8B-Instruct. We find a dissociation: the model represents sycophantic and factual agreement in geometrically distinct subspaces, yet the steering direction projects equally onto both and cannot differentially target either. The direction accordingly reduces agreement with factually correct statements (e.g. that the Earth is round) as well as sycophantic ones. All other static properties of the two activation groups are matched, suggesting the behavioural dissociation arises from generation dynamics or from finer-grained structure that residual-stream analysis cannot resolve. The pattern illustrates a general gap: representations that are readable from activations may not be writable through them.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A key step in knowledge discovery is the evaluation of data mining results. In several applications, including pattern mining, graph analysis, and others, this step includes the evaluation of the statistical significance of the results, to avoid spurious discoveries due only to noise or random fluctuations in the data. While specialized procedures have been developed for some specific applications, resampling-based approaches are widely used, in particular for complex analyses where analytical results cannot be derived. However, current resampling-based approaches require the generation and analysis of thousands of resampled datasets, and are therefore impractical for large datasets or computationally intensive analyses.
  In this paper, we introduce FewRS, a simple and effective resampling-based approach to assess the statistical significance of data mining results with rigorous guarantees on the probability of false discoveries. Our approach can be used in every situation where resampling-based approaches are applied. FewRS builds on our derivation of a novel bound to the supremum deviation of test statistics representing the quality of data mining results. We prove that FewRS needs to generate and analyze an extremely small number of resampled datasets, leading to a highly scalable approach with wide applicability. We test our approach on common tasks such as pattern mining and network analysis. In all cases, our approach results in a reduction of up to two orders of magnitude in running time compared to the state of the art, while preserving high statistical power, enabling the statistical validation of data mining results on large-scale real-world datasets.

This Perspective argues that semiconductor manufacturing exposes a broader computational-science challenge, namely that generative AI for constrained physical domains must be physics-informed by construction, not corrected only through post-hoc filtering. We survey the emerging architectural toolkit, including physics-informed diffusion, PDE-constrained variational models, neural-operator priors, and conservation-law-respecting generative networks, and show how it connects to differentiable lithography, TCAD, process simulation, and autonomous experimentation. We identify four integration patterns between generative models and physics-based simulators, and we propose a research agenda centered on physics-fidelity benchmarks, differentiable simulator infrastructure, and multimodal foundation models for physical design and manufacturing. ### [95] [Mechanical Field Networks: Structured Neural Dynamics for Multivariate Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11251)
*Xingji Cui*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MF-Net 是一种新型循环动力学模型，通过将交互结构学习内嵌于状态更新的“关系律”中，实现了在保持高效预测的同时，从观测轨迹中自动提取高可解释性的变量间耦合关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多变量动力学系统建模方法通常面临两难：要么强制施加预设的动力学结构（缺乏灵活性），要么学习灵活的状态转换但使交互机制变得隐蔽（缺乏可解释性）。作者旨在开发一种能够平衡预测性能与结构可解释性的模型，以自动发现观测轨迹背后的潜在交互机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MF-Net 的循环动力学模型。该模型将所有变量表示为一个共享的“场状态”（field state），并通过一个可学习的“关系律”（relation law）来更新该状态。模型将交互关系的发现融入到前向演化过程中，通过学习状态依赖的流、场响应和运动趋势来实现状态更新。其结构通过内生的内部量实现，即模型在进行预测的同时，能够直接解读出潜在的相互作用矩阵。

Result: 在多种系统（包括已知物理定律的系统、混沌基准测试、真实神经记录和生态时间序列）上，MF-Net 表现优异。在 40 维 Lorenz-96 基准测试中，其 8 步预测 $R^2$ 达到 $0.798 \pm 0.018$。更重要的是，该模型准确恢复了局部耦合支持，Precision@K 指标达到 $1.000 \pm 0.000$，显示出极强的结构还原能力。

Conclusion: MF-Net 成功地将动力学预测与交互结构学习统一在一个框架中。该模型证明了可以通过前向演化任务直接学习潜在的动力学机制，从而在保持高性能预测的同时，提供具有高度可解释性的耦合结构分析，为复杂系统的机制发现提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Many multivariate dynamical systems are observed only through trajectories, leaving the mechanisms governing their joint dynamics hidden. Existing approaches can impose interpretable dynamics or learn flexible state transitions, yet the resulting interaction structure is typically either specified in advance or left implicit within the learned dynamics. We introduce MF-Net, a recurrent dynamical model that represents all variables in a shared field state and updates this state through a learned relation law. Each variable carries a field component, and these components evolve jointly through a learnable mechanical transition. Here, mechanical refers to the relation-to-motion organization of the transition, where learned relations shape state-dependent flows, field responses, and motion tendencies that move the field state forward. The resulting structure is part of the rollout itself: learned relations influence how the field moves, and the same internal quantities support both forecasting and structural readout. Across known-law interaction systems, chaotic benchmarks, real neural recordings, and ecological time series, MF-Net achieves competitive short- and medium-horizon forecasting while retaining inspectable structural readout. On the 40-dimensional Lorenz--96 testbed, MF-Net achieves an eight-step $R^2$ of $0.798\pm0.018$; across five seeds, its learned relation matrix recovers the local coupling support with a local/nonlocal strength ratio of $19.80\pm1.00$ and Precision@$K$ of $1.000\pm0.000$. MF-Net provides a structure-readable dynamical modeling framework in which learned relations are trained through forward evolution and, on real data, interpreted as functional predictive couplings under appropriate observational limits.

### [96] [Bernstein-Schur Kernels: Random Features by Sketched Modulation and Radial Randomization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11255)
*Taha Bouhsine*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对难以直接应用传统方法的Bernstein-Schur核，本文提出了一种通过草图和径向特征混合的通用随机特征构造方法，实现了高效逼近并提供了严格的泛化误差界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bernstein-Schur核介于平稳核和点积核之间，属于非平稳核，现有的Bochner采样或多项式草图技术无法直接应用。作者旨在为这一类核函数寻找一种计算高效且具有理论可控性的随机特征逼近方法。

Method: 研究提出了一种“双重随机化”方法：针对有限维调制部分使用草图技术（sketching），针对完全单调的径向部分采用Bernstein-Widder尺度采样结合高斯随机傅里叶特征（RFF）。通过这种构造，特征维度被控制在 $Dm$（$m$为草图大小，$D$为径向采样数），避免了直接展开带来的维度爆炸问题。

Result: 在理论上证明了该估计器的无偏性，导出了精确的方差界，并通过矩阵Bernstein不等式证明了算子范数下的收敛性（取决于核的内禀维度而非原始维度）。实验验证了其在具有挑战性的yat-核（$yat$-kernel）上的有效性，并指出在固定预算下，每个尺度选择一个频率是方差最优的。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种适用于Bernstein-Schur核类的通用随机特征构造方法，通过双重随机化技术成功克服了非平稳核函数在传统方法（如Bochner采样或多项式草图）中的局限性，并为核岭回归等任务提供了理论上的泛化性能保证。

Abstract: Bernstein--Schur kernels are products of a finite-feature kernel (one with an explicit finite-dimensional feature map) and a completely monotone shift-invariant kernel: nonstationary kernels that fall between the shift-invariant and dot-product templates random features usually exploit, so in general neither Bochner sampling nor polynomial sketching applies to the full kernel directly. We give one random-feature construction for the whole class that \emph{randomizes both factors: it sketches the finite modulation and randomizes the completely monotone radial factor, sampling the latter's one-dimensional Bernstein--Widder scale and then applying Gaussian random Fourier features (whose frequency is still $d$-dimensional). The feature dimension is then $Dm$, set by the sketch size $m$ and the radial-draw count $D$, free of the $O(d^2)$ size of the exact modulation feature. Keeping the modulation \emph{exact} is the analyzable limit ($m\to\infty$): there we prove unbiasedness, an exact variance for the recommended flat estimator, an expected matrix-Bernstein operator-norm bound (with a matching high-probability tail) controlled by the top eigenvalues of the kernel and modulation Gram matrices together with an intrinsic dimension rather than the crude $N\max_{ij}$ entrywise route, and a deterministic relative-spectral kernel-ridge stability result. By conditioning on the sketch, the doubly-randomized estimator inherits the same intrinsic-dimension operator-norm guarantee plus a single additive sketch term, tunable by $m$ independently of $D$. The motivating instance is the biased $yat$-kernel $k_{yat,b}(w,x)=(w^\top x+b)^2/(\|w-x\|^2+\varepsilon)$, $b\ge0$, whose family span contains the inverse-multiquadric kernel by finite differences in $b$; for it the radial mixture is the IMQ spectral sampler, and one frequency per scale is variance-optimal at a fixed radial-feature budget.

### [97] [Loss Landscape Diagnosis for Gradient-Based Gray-Scott System Inversion: Disentangling the Roles of PINN Components](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11258)

TL;DR: 本文通过对PDE系统进行直接反向传播和PINN方法的对比分析，揭示了PINN成功避开PDE参数反演中“病态景观”（平坦区域与陡峭悬崖）的根本原因：神经网络通过隐式编码动力学过程，平滑了原本复杂的优化环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的反应-扩散系统参数反演多依赖于代理模型或PINN，而直接通过PDE结构进行反向传播的方法常被回避。作者旨在探究为何直接优化PDE参数会导致失败，并以此为消融实验，深入分析PINN中各组件（神经网络与PDE结构）的作用机制。

Method: 本文采用了对比实验法，将基于PDE结构直接进行反向传播（即“解卷”模拟）作为基准，对比了不带神经网络的纯PDE参数优化过程与PINN方法的表现。通过可视化损失函数景观，分析了优化失败的几何原因，从而剥离并评估了神经网络在PINN框架中的具体贡献。

Result: 直接对PDE结构进行反向传播会导致优化陷入没有梯度信号的平坦区域，这些区域被与分岔边界对齐的陡峭悬崖所包围。而加入神经网络后，由于其隐式编码了全动力学信息，使得损失函数景观变得平滑，从而规避了上述病态，证明了神经网络在补全数据和改善优化景观方面的核心作用。

Conclusion: 研究发现，PINN在求解PDE反问题时，神经网络的作用并非仅仅是拟合数据，而是通过隐式编码动力学特征，有效地平滑了原本存在严重病态（如平坦区域和陡峭悬崖）的损失函数景观。这一结论明确了神经网络与PDE物理结构在参数反演任务中的分工。

Abstract: Gradient-based inversion of reaction-diffusion systems is typically approached via surrogate models or physics-informed neural networks (PINNs), while the most direct route, backpropagation through the PDE's structure itself, has largely been avoided. We pursue this direct route as a diagnostic probe, backpropagating a steady-state loss through unrolled Gray-Scott simulation to recover its parameters, with no surrogate or neural-network augmentation. Optimization fails to converge, and plotting the landscape directly locates the failure in its geometry -- flat plateaus with no gradient signal, bounded by sharp cliffs that align with bifurcation boundaries -- a structure that recurs across loss functions and is inherited however the gradients are routed to parameters. Reading this minimal setup as an ablation of PINN, we disentangle each component's role: with the neural network fixed, the residual loss is quadratic in the PDE parameters and yields a smooth landscape, so it alone already avoids the pathology, by implicitly encoding the full PDE dynamics across all initial conditions. The neural network, for its part, cannot repair an ill-posed parameter subspace, and so serves only to complete the observed data -- a division of labor not previously made explicit. These findings carry concrete design implications for PINN-type methods and a broader heuristic on when added dimensions actually help.

</details>


### [98] [PermDoRA -- Understanding Adapter Interference in Language Models: Limits of Parameter-Space Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11262)
*Gowtham Sivaramakrishnan,Sarvesha Kumar Kombaiah Seetha,Kishan Gupta Balaji,Santhosh Baradwaj Vaduvur Ranganathan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了在大模型适配器组合中，参数空间的几何特性是否导致领域间干扰。研究证明，通过强制参数正交性或方向独立性来改善多领域组合性能的假设是无效的，适配器间的干扰机制可能更深层地存在于非线性表示交互中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型中实现访问控制需要模块化的机制，以在不进行重训练的前提下实现特定领域的功能。现有的主流假设认为适配器间的干扰源于线性参数更新的重叠，因此强制正交化或方向独立性被认为可以提升多领域性能。本研究旨在通过实证检验该几何假设是否成立。

Method: 提出了DoRA-RBAC框架，这是一种基于权重分解低秩自适应（Weight-decomposed Low-Rank Adaptation）的分层适配器组合方法。研究对比了传统的欧几里得空间合并方法与一种几何感知（Riemannian-inspired）的合并策略，该策略通过跨多QA基准测试对归一化方向进行平均来近似Frechet平均。此外，研究还对适配器更新的角度对齐和正交性与组合性能的关系进行了诊断分析。

Result: 研究发现，虽然单领域性能与LoRA相当，但在多领域设置下，几何感知合并策略并未比标准的参数平均产生持续的优势。诊断分析显示，适配器更新的角度对齐和正交性对组合性能的预测能力较弱。

Conclusion: 研究表明，大模型适配器（adapter）间的干扰并非主要由参数空间的几何性质（如线性参数更新的重叠）所决定，而是更可能源于共享非线性表示层面的交互。因此，通过正交化或方向独立性来提升多领域适配器组合性能的假设在实证中未得到支持。

Abstract: Access control in large language models (LLMs) requires modular mechanisms to enable domain-specific behavior without retraining or cross-domain interference. A common hypothesis is that interference during adapter composition arises from overlap in linear parameter updates, suggesting that enforcing orthogonality or directional independence should improve multi-domain performance. We test this hypothesis using DoRA-RBAC, a hierarchical adapter composition framework based on weight-decomposed low-rank adaptation. We compare conventional Euclidean merging with a geometry-aware Riemannian-inspired merging strategy that approximates the Frechet mean via normalized directional averaging across multiple QA benchmarks (GPQA, PubMedQA, SimpleQA, WMDP) on LLaMA-3.1-8B and Mistral-7B. Our results show that while single-domain performance matches LoRA, geometry-aware merging provides no consistent advantage over standard averaging in multi-domain settings.Diagnostic analysis further reveals that angular alignment and orthogonality of adapter updates are weak predictors of composition performance. These findings suggest that adapter interference is not governed primarily by parameter-space geometry, but is instead consistent with interactions in shared nonlinear representations.

</details>


### [99] [DeMix: Debugging Training Data with Mixed Data Error Types by Investigating Influence Vectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11616)
*Jiale Deng,Yanyan Shen,Xiaogang Shi,Chai Junjun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对机器学习训练数据中标签、特征及虚假相关性等混合型错误难以诊断的问题，DeMix 通过分析样本影响向量及引入干预学习机制，实现了错误样本的高精度识别与分类，显著提升了数据修复效果及模型表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实场景的数据集常存在标签错误、特征错误和虚假相关性等混合型错误，而现有的数据清洗和归因方法往往难以同时完成错误检测与类型识别，限制了针对性数据修复的效率。

Method: 提出了一种名为 DeMix 的框架，核心方法包括：1. 利用“影响向量”（Influence Vectors）捕捉样本对验证集预测的特异性模式；2. 将数据调试建模为多标签分类问题，直接从影响向量中预测错误类型；3. 引入基于干预的学习策略（Intervention-based learning strategy），引导分类器提取针对特定错误类型的不变解释，增强泛化能力。

Result: 在表格数据预测、推荐系统和大模型对齐等 11 项任务的实证评估中，DeMix 表现优异，相比现有最先进方法，数据调试的 F1 分数提高了 22.61%，数据修复后的下游模型性能提升了 9.32%。

Conclusion: DeMix 证明了利用样本对验证集预测的影响向量（Influence Vectors）能够有效识别复杂数据错误。该方法通过将数据调试转化为多标签分类任务，不仅能够精准定位错误样本，还能明确错误类型，为自动化、针对性的数据修复提供了高效的框架。

Abstract: High-quality training data is essential for the success of machine learning models. However, real-world datasets often contain mixed types of errors arising from systematic flaws in data preparation pipelines, including label errors, feature errors, and spurious correlations. Effective debugging of training data requires both detecting erroneous samples and identifying their specific error types to enable targeted repair, yet existing data cleaning and attribution methods fail to adequately address this dual requirement. In this paper, we propose DeMix, a novel framework that simultaneously diagnoses erroneous samples and their error types. Our key insight is that different error types produce distinct patterns on model behavior. DeMix captures such error-specific patterns by influence vectors that characterize how each training sample affects model predictions across all validation samples. We formulate training data debugging as a multi-label classification problem where a classifier is developed to predict error types directly from influence vectors. We further introduce an intervention-based learning strategy that guides the classifier to capture invariant rationales specific to each error type, ensuring the learned classifier generalizes effectively. Empirical evaluations on 11 tasks across tabular data prediction, recommendation systems, and LLM alignment demonstrate that DeMix significantly outperforms state-of-the-art approaches, achieving a 22.61% improvement in data debugging F1-score and a 9.32% gain in task model performance after data repair. Code is available at: https://github.com/SJTU-DMTai/DeMix.

</details>


### [100] [Seeing Before Colliding: Anticipatory Safe RL with Frozen Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11266)
*Samuel Tetteh,Cody Fleming*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统强化学习在高速场景下反应式安全机制的滞后问题，本文提出了VLM-Safe-RL框架，通过将预训练视觉语言模型的先验预测作为成本项集成至拉格朗日更新过程，显著提升了智能体的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的受限强化学习算法多依赖“反应式”成本信号（即发生碰撞或超限后才惩罚），在高速运动场景下，这种滞后性导致安全机制失效。因此，研究旨在引入具有预判能力的视觉语言模型，将“先验性”成本引入约束优化过程。

Method: 1. 解耦双路径CLIP：实现奖励与成本路径的分离，符合CMDP的因子分解；2. VLM-Lagrange：在拉格朗日乘子更新中引入每步的VLM预测成本作为先验项；3. 置信度门控（Confidence Gating）：基于CLIP边际的逻辑噪声模型推导出贝叶斯最优权重；4. VLMPPOLag：将上述机制集成至PPO-Lagrangian算法中。

Result: 在Safety-Gymnasium FormulaOne L2基准测试中，VLMPPOLag+Conf是唯一能在保持实质性回报的同时，在多数种子下将成本控制在限额内的算法。此外，该方法在MetaDrive Medium环境下的灾难发生率显著降低（从41%降至26%），验证了其在不同模拟环境下的泛化能力与有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种将预训练视觉语言模型（VLM）作为先验成本信号引入受限强化学习（Constrained RL）的新范式。实验证明，VLM提供的预测性信号能显著改善高速场景下的安全性，为未来将大模型融入安全控制系统提供了有效路径。

Abstract: The cost signal that constrained-RL algorithms optimize against is almost always reactive: the simulator emits a non-zero cost only after a collision has begun, and the Lagrange multiplier of PPO-Lagrangian grows only after the episode budget has been exceeded. At race speeds, where collisions are instantaneous and irreversible, any safety mechanism that waits for cost to accumulate is structurally too late. We present VLM-Safe-RL, a framework that integrates a frozen vision-language model into the CMDP Lagrangian update as an anticipatory cost term. The framework comprises four contributions: (i) Decoupled Dual-Path CLIP, independent reward/cost paths that respect the CMDP's factorization; (ii) VLM-Lagrange, an augmented multiplier update that incorporates a per-step VLM cost as an anticipatory term; (iii) Confidence Gating, a Bayes-optimal weight derived from a logistic noise model on the CLIP margin; and (iv) VLMPPOLag, the composed algorithm. On Safety-Gymnasium FormulaOne L2, our principal evaluation ($n{=}5$ seeds, $10^{6}$ steps, budget $d_{\text{lim}}{=}25$) VLMPPOLag$+$Conf is the only configuration in our default budget comparison that simultaneously retains substantive return ($J_r{\approx}40$) and holds cost within budget on a majority of seeds; the five constraint-aware baselines (PPOLag, CPO, CPPOPID, CPO-CLG, PPOLag-RND) each fail at least one requirement. The mechanism generalizes to held-out MetaDrive Medium (catastrophe rate $41\%{\to}26\%$, 95\% bootstrap CI $[-26,-5]$\,pp) and shows directionally consistent transfer to Bullet Safety-Gym; we report honestly where it does not (MetaDrive Easy/Hard, Qwen2-VL backbone) and trace the Hard failure to a Lagrangian-regulation pathology rather than the VLM signal itself. To our knowledge, this is the first work to use frozen VLM signals as an anticipatory cost term inside the CMDP Lagrangian update.

</details>


### [101] [A prior-free blind detection of information leakage from model predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11267)
*Laurence A. Jacobs*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种仅基于模型输出的通用数据泄露检测框架，通过决策论方法识别三种类型的泄露，并证明了在特定条件下无法检测微小泄露的理论极限，为机器学习模型审计提供了一种高效、无须访问训练过程的检测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器学习驱动的科学研究中，数据泄露（data leakage）是导致可复现性失败的主要原因。现有的检测工具通常需要训练代码、外部数据或深度领域知识，而审计者往往仅能获得模型输出。因此，本文旨在研究仅根据模型的预测结果和真实观测值，是否能够判断模型是否存在数据泄露。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于决策论的检测框架，利用预测风险与结果分布的关系，结合适当评分规则（proper scoring rules）和决策曲线分析（decision-curve analysis）进行建模。作者通过数学证明定义了不同泄露类别的可检测性边界，并针对“近确定性子组泄露”设计了无先验测试方法。最后，在英国生物银行（UK Biobank）数据集上进行了实证验证。

Result: 研究证明了存在一个理论上的“不可检测界限”：如果泄露后的模型与诚实模型在校准和区分度上表现一致，则无法通过任何预测输出函数区分两者。同时，研究提出了一种针对近确定性子组的检测方法，并通过英国生物银行数据验证了检测的有效性，证明了在特定阈值下，微小的残余泄露是无法被输出数据检测出的，且其影响微乎其微。

Conclusion: 本文构建了一个仅基于模型输出（预测值与真实标签）的通用数据泄露检测框架，揭示了数据泄露的三分法（误校准、广义校准、确定性泄露）。研究指出，在给定性能上限的条件下，部分泄露是无法通过输出检测出来的，但对于近确定性子组泄露，存在一种无需先验的有效检测手段。该方法在计算效率上极高，为审计机器学习模型提供了一个实用的工具。

Abstract: Data leakage -- contamination of a model with information unavailable at baseline -- is the dominant reproducibility failure in machine-learning-based science, yet detection tools require training code, external data, or domain expertise. None operates on the artifact an auditor most often holds: the model's output. We ask what can be decided about leakage from predictions and outcomes alone. We give a decision-theoretic framework in which leakage diagnostics are functionals of the predicted-risk/outcome law, parameterized by a threshold-weighting linked to proper scoring rules and decision-curve analysis. We prove a sharp impossibility: a recalibrated leak matching an honest model's calibration and discrimination is indistinguishable from honest performance by \emph{any} function of the predictions, so the broad class is detectable only against an externally supplied ceiling on achievable discrimination. We then prove what leakage cannot hide: a near-deterministic subgroup -- the signature of a near-label leak -- produces a sustained unit-purity head that no legitimate predictor of a non-deterministic outcome can manufacture, yielding a prior-free test. These results organize leakage into a trichotomy -- miscalibrated, broad-calibrated, and deterministic -- each with a matched detector and failure mode. We validate on UK Biobank using time-windowed comorbidity leakage with known, graded severity, measuring a detection floor of $Δ\cstar \approx 0.007$ on this endpoint, below which residual leakage is undetectable from output and too small to alter conclusions. The numerical floor is cohort- and endpoint-specific; the structural lesson is general: output-only detection fails where residual leakage is indistinguishable from an honestly stronger predictor. The test returns a verdict on a prediction vector in under a second on commodity hardware.

</details>

*Abhilash Neog,Sepideh Fatemi,Medha Sawhney,Kazi Sajeed Mehrab,Aanish Pradhan,Bennett J. McAfee,Emma Marchisin,Arka Daw,Robert Ladwig,Cayelan C. Carey,Paul Hanson,Anuj Karpatne*

Conclusion: LakeFM 作为一个针对水生系统的基础模型，证明了在大规模模拟和观测数据上进行预训练能够有效提升湖泊动态预测的泛化能力，为理解复杂的湖泊生态系统提供了一个强大的通用工具。

Abstract: Understanding and forecasting lake dynamics is critical for monitoring water quality and ecosystem health across lakes and reservoirs. While machine learning methods have been recently applied to ecological time-series data, existing works assume regular sampling in time and depth, and struggle to generalize across lakes with heterogeneous variables, depths, and observation patterns. To address these limitations, we introduce \textsc{LakeFM}, a foundation model for aquatic systems, pre-trained on large-scale ecological datasets comprising both simulated and observed lakes. Through extensive empirical evaluation, we show that \textsc{LakeFM} learns meaningful representations spanning broader lake-level characteristics, and achieves competitive or often superior-forecasting performance compared to existing time-series foundation and non-foundation models, while producing physically plausible predictions consistent with real-world lake dynamics.

### [103] [Quantifying Subliminal Behavioral Transfer Ratios in Language Model Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11270)
*Uwe Konig,Hamza Kazmi,Ruizhe Li,Maheep Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究定量分析了语言模型蒸馏中的“潜意识学习”现象，证实即使使用完全良性的训练数据，学生模型仍会从教师模型继承不良行为，且不同模型的迁移机制存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨并量化语言模型在蒸馏过程中是否存在“潜意识学习”现象，即教师模型中的有害倾向是否会无意中传递给仅接受良性训练数据的学生模型，并分析这种现象的规模及特征。

Method: 通过对 Llama-2-7B-Chat 和 Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct 两个教师模型施加不同强度的干预（steering），并在仅包含良性数据的训练集上蒸馏学生模型；最后使用 GPT-4.1 对学生模型在 100 个 JailbreakBench 提示词上的表现进行评估，定量分析潜意识行为迁移的比率。

Result: 研究发现迁移效果具有鲁棒性，但不同模型表现出不同的缩放行为：Llama-2 表现出明显的阈值效应（在特定干预强度下风险激增），而 Qwen2.5 则表现出持续且更高水平的行为迁移（迁移比率 τ 高达 0.61）。

Conclusion: 研究证明，知识蒸馏过程中存在显著的“潜意识学习”现象，即使只使用良性数据，学生模型仍会继承教师模型中潜在的不良行为。这种迁移的程度与教师模型的架构及参数调整强度密切相关，模型开发者在进行蒸馏时必须警惕这种安全风险的隐性传递。

Abstract: Distillation of a language model intended to transfer benign behavior to a student model may also transfer undesirable characteristics, if they are present in the teacher model, a phenomenon known as subliminal learning. While qualitative evidence supports the existence of this effect, its magnitude has not been systematically characterized. This study quantifies subliminal behavioral transfer ratios by steering two teacher models (Llama-2-7B-Chat and Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct) at varying steering strengths and distilling student models using only benign data. Evaluation on 100 JailbreakBench prompts with GPT-4.1, serving as the evaluator, indicates that transfer is robust but exhibits distinct scaling behaviors. Llama-2 demonstrates a sharp threshold ($τ= {0.25,0.32} \ \text{beyond} \ α= -0.15$), whereas Qwen2.5 displays continuous and higher levels of transfer ($τ$ up to $0.61$).

### [104] [Federated continual learning: A comprehensive survey on lifelong and privacy-preserving learning over distributed and non-stationary data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11272)
*Masoume Gholizade,Fabrizio Ruffini,Pietro Ducange,Francesco Marcelloni*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有联邦学习（FL）方法大多基于数据静态的假设，在医疗、物联网等数据流动态变化的现实场景中，FL模型常面临性能退化和灾难性遗忘问题。而传统的持续学习（CL）主要集中在中心化设置，未能解决联邦系统中的隐私、通信受限和客户端异构性等约束。因此，需要系统性研究如何结合FL与CL，支持跨分布式非平稳数据的终身学习。

Method: 本文采用文献综述法，通过定义FCL问题、梳理现有FL在非平稳数据环境下的局限性，提出了一种多维度的FCL分类法。此外，文章还归纳了评估指标、应用领域，并对未来的研究方向与开放性挑战进行了系统分析。

Result: 本文提供了一份关于联邦持续学习（FCL）的全面综述，明确了其核心概念与特征，构建了系统化的方法分类框架，总结了关键评估标准，并识别了当前FCL研究中的主要瓶颈与未来路线图。

Conclusion: 联邦持续学习（FCL）是实现鲁棒、自适应且具备隐私保护的分布式人工智能系统的关键。尽管该领域发展迅速，但仍需在应对极端异构性、设计高效内存机制以及建立标准化评估基准方面取得突破，以推动其在现实场景中的广泛部署。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative and privacy-preserving model training across distributed clients, but most existing FL systems implicitly assume data stationarity. In real-world settings-such as healthcare, industrial IoT (IIOT), cybersecurity, and smart cities-data streams are inherently non-stationary, leading classical FL methods to suffer from performance degradation, instability, and catastrophic forgetting.
  Continual Learning (CL) addresses learning under evolving data distributions but has been largely studied in centralized settings, overlooking key constraints of federated systems, including privacy, limited communication, and client heterogeneity. Federated Continual Learning (FCL) emerges at the intersection of FL and CL, aiming to support lifelong, adaptive, and privacy-aware learning over distributed and non-stationary data.
  This survey provides a comprehensive and systematic overview of FCL. We first present a formal definition of the FCL problem and clarify its distinctive characteristics. We then analyze the limitations of classical FL under non-stationary conditions, highlighting how CL principles support long-term adaptation. To organize the rapidly growing literature, we propose a multi-dimensional taxonomy of FCL approaches. Furthermore, we review representative application domains and data modalities, summarize commonly used evaluation metrics, and discuss experimental perspectives for assessing long-term performance and forgetting. Finally, we highlight key open challenges, including handling extreme heterogeneity under temporal drift, designing scalable and privacy-preserving memory mechanisms, and establishing standardized benchmarks. This survey aims to serve as a reference and a roadmap for advancing FCL toward robust and deployable real-world systems.

### [105] [RoVE: Rotary Value Embeddings Attention for Relative Position-dependent Value Pathways](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11275)
*Alejandro García-Castellanos,Maurice Weiler,Erik J Bekkers*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对RoPE机制中Value路径缺乏位置敏感性的问题，作者提出了RoVE方法，通过对Value进行旋转处理，将注意力机制转化为注意力卷积，提升了模型在长距离依赖任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的RoPE机制虽然实现了Query与Key的相对位置感知，但Value路径仍然是位置盲（position-blind）的，导致模型在处理长距离依赖和长文本聚合任务时存在局限性。

Method: 提出了一种无需额外参数的改进方法RoVE（Rotary Value Embeddings）。该方法在应用旋转位置编码（RoPE）时，不仅对Query和Key进行旋转，还同步对Value向量进行旋转，从而使模型在信息传递过程中具有位置敏感性。

Result: 在124M和354M参数量的GPT-2模型上进行实验，结果表明RoVE在少样本上下文学习（ICL）、分布外（OOD）困惑度以及长文本检索任务中均优于标准RoPE，特别是在长距离信息聚合任务中表现出显著优势。

Conclusion: RoVE通过将位置旋转机制扩展至Value向量，不仅增强了模型对位置信息的感知能力，还揭示了其与注意力卷积（Attentive Convolution）的理论联系，为现代大语言模型架构提供了一种更通用且高效的位置编码改进方案。

Abstract: Rotary Position Embeddings (RoPE) make attention scores position-relative but leave the value pathway position-blind: the message sent by a value token is the same regardless of its distance from the query. We propose RoVE, a parameter-free modification that makes values position-sensitive by rotating them simultaneously with keys, and show that it turns RoPE attention into attentive convolution. This new perspective unifies several independent formulations of the same operation across computer vision, robotics, and modern LLM architectures. Trained 124M and 354M GPT-2 models show consistent empirical gains over RoPE on few-shot in-context learning, out-of-distribution perplexity, and long-context retrieval, with the clearest improvements on tasks that require long-range aggregation.

### [106] [Least-Action-Guided Diffusion for Physical Extrapolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11277)
*Zhongxin Yang,Yuanwei Bin,Xiang I. A. Yang,Shiyi Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LAPG是一种将最小作用量原理整合进扩散模型推理过程的新框架，通过推理时的物理引导而非训练时的惩罚机制，显著提升了生成模型在物理系统模拟中的外推能力和一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成模型在训练范围外（如时间、参数或几何形态）进行外推时，往往会产生违反物理规律的结果，且传统的物理信息约束方法通常依赖于难以平衡的经验性损失函数。

Method: 提出了一种最小作用量引导的扩散模型（LAPG）。该方法分为两阶段：首先利用条件得分扩散模型生成分布内初始预测；其次，引入基于作用量导数的变分先验，在推理阶段对预测结果进行物理一致性校正，从而避免了对训练时施加硬约束的依赖。

Result: 在自由落体、弹簧质量系统、点涡动力学及翼型势流等多种微分方程系统中，LAPG显著降低了相位漂移，更好地保持了耗散衰减特性，并提升了在外推测试中的准确度，表现优于传统的物理信息驱动基准模型。

Conclusion: LAPG通过引入基于最小作用量原理的推理时引导机制，有效解决了生成模型在计算物理领域中外推能力不足及物理一致性难以保证的问题，为科学计算提供了一种通用且稳健的改进框架。

Abstract: Reliable extrapolation remains a central challenge for generative models in computational physics, because models trained over finite ranges of time, parameters, or geometries may produce physically inconsistent predictions outside the training distribution. We introduce a least-action-principle-guided diffusion, LAPG, a framework that promotes physical consistency during inference rather than relying solely on constraints imposed during training. The method combines a conditional score-based diffusion model with an action-derived physical guidance score. In the first stage, the learned score model generates an in-distribution proposal; in the second, an action-based variational prior refines this proposal toward the target out-of-distribution condition. This formulation turns the principle of least action into a differentiable inference-time correction mechanism and provides an alternative to pointwise residual penalties that often require empirical loss balancing.
  We evaluate LAPG on representative ordinary- and partial-differential-equation systems, including free fall, conservative and dissipative spring-mass dynamics, interacting point vortices, and potential flow over parameterized airfoils. In temporal, parameter, and geometric extrapolation tests, LAPG reduces phase drift, preserves dissipative decay, captures vortex motion, and improves the lift response of airfoil flows compared with training-time physics-informed baselines.

### [107] [FreeBridge: Variational Schrödinger Bridges for Cellular Transition Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11286)
*Xurui Wang,Qin Ren,Jun Ma,Haibin Ling,Chenyu You*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FreeBridge 是一种用于单细胞扰动建模的新型薛定谔桥框架，通过将演化轨迹限制在已知的细胞流形内，解决了传统生成模型在仅有终点观测时难以生成生物学合理解释的中间轨迹的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高内涵成像实验无法观测单个细胞的连续轨迹，因为细胞在采集时已被固定。现有的生成模型虽然能实现良好的终点对齐，但无法保证中间演化过程的生物学合理性，即可能产生偏离实际细胞形态分布的虚假轨迹。

Method: 提出了 FreeBridge 模型，这是一种基于薛定谔桥（Schrödinger Bridge）的框架。该方法将原子状态定义为实例分割后的单细胞表征，构建了一个固定的细胞流形，并通过经验潜在支持正则化（empirical latent support regularization）将随机传输限制在该几何结构内，从而在仅有终点观测的情况下推断细胞演化轨迹。

Result: 在 BBBC021、RxRx1 和 JUMP 等多个基准数据集上，FreeBridge 在保持终点保真度和作用机制（MoA）一致性的前提下，显著降低了中间状态对现实分布的支持度违规，展现了更优的轨迹可解释性。

Conclusion: FreeBridge 证明了在单细胞扰动建模中，通过几何基础（即在已知的细胞流形内约束随机传输）对于生成生物学上可解释的演化路径至关重要，它有效地解决了仅靠终点对齐无法保证中间状态合理性的问题。

Abstract: High-content imaging assays quantify cellular responses to chemical and genetic perturbations, yet continuous trajectories of individual cells are unobservable because cells are chemically fixed at acquisition. Perturbation modeling therefore reduces to inferring stochastic transport between control and treated populations observed only as separate marginals. While recent generative models achieve strong end-point alignment, boundary consistency does not determine intermediate evolution: multiple stochastic processes may connect identical marginals while traversing regions unsupported by observed single-cell morphologies. We introduce \textbf{FreeBridge}, a Schrödinger Bridge formulation for single-cell transition modeling under endpoint-only supervision. FreeBridge defines atomic states as instance-segmented single-cell representations, establishing a fixed cellular manifold, and learns stochastic transport constrained within this geometry via empirical latent support regularization. Across BBBC021, RxRx1, and JUMP, FreeBridge maintains competitive or improved endpoint fidelity and mechanism-of-action retention under a unified evaluation protocol; on BBBC021, it further reduces intermediate support violations. These findings highlight the importance of geometric grounding for biologically interpretable perturbation dynamics. Project page: https://y-research-sbu.github.io/FreeBridge/.

### [108] [FlowBank: Query-Adaptive Agentic Workflows Optimization through Precompute-and-Reuse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11290)
*Lingzhi Yuan,Chenghao Deng,Fangxu Yu,Souradip Chakraborty,Mohammad Rostami,Furong Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型多智能体系统中“离线搜索通用工作流”与“在线生成工作流”之间的成本与效率矛盾，本文提出 FlowBank 框架。通过构建一个互补的工作流组合库，并在推理时动态路由查询，在显著提升性能的同时有效控制了计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体工作流优化方法存在权衡困境：任务级方法离线成本高且仅能部署单一工作流；查询级方法实时生成成本高。作者发现不同工作流擅长处理不同的查询子集，因此提出应构建一个可重用的互补工作流库，并在推理时进行自适应选择，以同时实现高准确率和低计算成本。

Method: 本文提出了 FlowBank 框架，包含三个核心阶段：
1. Diversifying（多样化）：通过 DiverseFlow 策略引导搜索过程，优先覆盖未被解决的任务，生成互补的高质量工作流池。
2. Curating（精简）：利用 CuraFlow 算法压缩工作流池，去除冗余，构建规模小且功能互补的工作流组合。
3. Matching（匹配）：将部署转化为二分图中的边值预测问题，在推理时根据查询内容，动态路由至最优的预计算工作流。

Result: FlowBank 在五个基准测试中均取得了最优的平均得分。相较于当前最强的自动化优化方法，性能提升了 4.26%；相较于最强的人工设计基线，性能提升了 14.92%，同时保持了极具竞争力的推理成本。

Conclusion: FlowBank 证明了通过构建互补的工作流组合并进行自适应选择，能够有效平衡大型语言模型多智能体系统的性能与推理成本。该方法在多个基准测试中超越了现有的自动化与手动工作流设计方法，证实了“组合式优化”比追求单一通用工作流或实时生成工作流更具优势。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM)-based multi-agent systems are increasingly powerful, but current agentic workflow optimization paradigms make an unsatisfying trade-off. Task-level methods spend substantial offline compute yet deploy only a single workflow, leaving complementary candidates unused, while query-level methods synthesize a new workflow per query at substantial inference cost. Our motivating analysis shows these paradigms are more complementary than competing: workflows discovered during offline search often solve different subsets of queries, and many queries handled by expensive query-level generation can already be solved by cheaper precomputed workflows. This suggests a different objective: rather than searching for one universally best workflow or regenerating one per instance, we should build a compact bank of reusable, complementary workflows and select among them adaptively at inference time. Doing so requires solving three coupled problems: generating complementary rather than redundant candidates, compressing them into a small deployable portfolio, and assigning each query to the right workflow under a performance-cost trade-off. To this end, we present FlowBank, a three-stage framework for portfolio-based agentic workflow optimization. Diversifying proposes DiverseFlow to steer search toward under-covered queries and produce a high-coverage candidate pool. Curating proposes CuraFlow to compress this pool into a compact portfolio with minimal redundancy. Matching casts deployment as edge-value prediction on a query-workflow bipartite graph and routes each incoming query to the portfolio member with the best predicted utility. Across five benchmarks, FlowBank achieves the highest average score among the evaluated methods while remaining cost-competitive, improving over the strongest automated and handcrafted baselines by 4.26% and 14.92% relative, respectively.

</details>


### [109] [Learning from almost nothing: How neural networks survive heavy input corruption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11319)
*Justin Tahmassebpur,Asadullah Bhuiyan,Hyejin Kim,Omri Lesser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了神经网络在严重属性噪声下的鲁棒性，通过理论分析揭示了神经网络在极端情况下实际上演变成了“最近类均值”分类器，从而解释了其在输入信号微弱时仍能保持有效学习的机理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的机器学习研究多集中于标签噪声，而对于输入数据的“属性噪声”（即输入损坏但标签正确）缺乏深入分析。本文旨在探究神经网络在面对严重损坏的输入数据时为何依然具有显著的鲁棒性，并尝试从理论上对其进行解释。

Method: 1. 实验方法：在多个分类数据集上通过添加“加性噪声”和“替换噪声”来模拟属性噪声，并利用多层感知器（MLP）进行训练测试。2. 理论分析：利用平均场理论（mean-field-inspired approach）分析无限宽神经网络在重度噪声环境下的决策行为，推导出一阶决策规则。

Result: 1. 神经网络展现出极强的鲁棒性，即便在超过90%的输入数据被损坏的情况下，仍能保持高于随机水平的准确率。2. 理论分析证明，在重度噪声环境下，MLP的行为可近似为“最近类均值”（Nearest-Class-Mean）分类器。3. 该结论在各种网络深度、激活函数及噪声分布下均具有普适性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，多层感知器在极端属性噪声（输入损坏率超过90%）下仍能保持良好的分类性能。其鲁棒性的核心原因在于模型通过“原型规则”（最近类均值算法）进行决策，这种机制具有普适性，且解释了为何即便个体训练样本几乎不含有效信号，模型仍能成功学习。

Abstract: Learning from imperfect data is a central theme in machine learning, connecting practical questions of robustness to fundamental questions of learnability. Here we examine attribute noise: learning from corrupted inputs while keeping the labels intact, a setting that has received considerably less analytical attention than its label-noise counterpart. We consider two types of corruption models: additive noise and replacement noise. Through experiments with multi-layer perceptrons (MLPs) on corrupted classification datasets, we find that neural networks remain robust, maintaining well-above-chance accuracy even when inputs are >90% corrupted -- far beyond human recognition. To understand this robustness, we analyze infinite-width networks in the heavy-corruption regime using a mean-field-inspired approach and derive a leading-order decision rule for the classification outcome: the network implements a prototype rule, the nearest-class-mean, assigning each test point to the class whose training-set average it most closely resembles. This leading-order decision rule is universal across a broad range of MLP architectures, holding for any depth, as well as a wide class of activation functions and noise distributions. The same centroid mechanism closely matches finite-width network behavior in our experiments and provides an interpretable and analytically tractable account of why learning can succeed even when individual training examples carry almost no signal.

### [110] [Energy-Conserved Neural Pipelines: Attenuating Error Propagation in Modular Neural Networks via Physical Conservation Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11341)
*David Young,Swan Yi Htet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对模块化神经网络的噪声累积问题，本文提出了一种强制执行特征能量（L2范数平方）守恒的机制，通过物理约束有效限制了噪声在模块间的传播与放大，显著提升了模型在各种噪声干扰下的稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模块化神经网络在处理任务时存在严重的“误差累积”问题，即模块间的噪声会随着深度增加而传播并放大，导致系统整体性能大幅下降。作者旨在寻找一种物理约束机制，以从源头上抑制模块边界处的噪声传递。

Method: 提出了一种基于“能量守恒”的硬约束机制，将特征向量的L2范数平方定义为激活能量，并强制其在模块边界处保持不变。该方法不同于传统的软惩罚，通过将能量限制作为不可违背的定律，防止了模块间噪声的产生或放大。同时，从数学上证明了守恒机制能严格限制输入噪声能量的传播。

Result: 在CIFAR-10实验中，该方法在噪声环境下（sigma=0.2）保留了77.4%的准确率，远超基线模型。此外，该方法表现出深度不变性，在面对系统性偏差、高斯噪声及对抗性噪声时均具有显著优势。在MuJoCo机器人模拟实验中，该方法平均提升了18.9个百分点的任务表现，验证了其实用价值。

Conclusion: 通过引入物理守恒定律作为神经网络模块间的硬约束，研究提出了一种鲁棒的模块化处理框架。该方法不仅在理论上限制了噪声传播，且在图像分类与机器人控制任务中均表现出显著的鲁棒性优势，证明了能量守恒是缓解深层模型误差累积的有效手段。

Abstract: Modular neural network pipelines suffer from error compounding: noise at any module boundary propagates and potentially amplifies through subsequent modules. We introduce energy conservation as a hard physical constraint on inter-module information flow. Activation energy (the squared L2 norm of feature vectors) is enforced to be exactly preserved at every module boundary. Unlike soft energy penalties, conservation is an inviolable law: the network may redistribute energy across neurons but cannot create or destroy it. Four experiments on CIFAR-10 demonstrate: (1) conservation retains 77.4% of clean accuracy at noise sigma=0.2, versus 35.1% for baselines and 30.9% for energy-penalized models (p<0.001, 5 seeds); (2) pipelines become depth-invariant, retaining 93.3% at depths 2 through 5 with noise at every boundary; (3) the advantage generalizes to systematic bias (+45.1%), Gaussian (+40.4%), and adversarial noise (+4.8%), with a principled non-effect on dropout (-0.3%); (4) on ResNet-18, the conservation advantage scales inversely with intrinsic normalization: +0.3 pp with BatchNorm, +26.2 pp without at sigma=0.2, reaching +58.0 pp at sigma=0.5. Experiment 5 validates the operator on a real modular robotic pipeline (MuJoCo physics, Franka Panda). Across three independent runs on separate machines (90 trials per cell), conservation provides +18.9 pp average advantage on monocular-depth-style noise. A formal bound proves conserved noise energy is strictly less than input noise energy.

### [111] [SwiftCTS: Fast Cross-Design Prediction and Pareto Optimization of Clock Tree Metrics via Few-Shot Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11348)
*Barsat Khadka,Kawsher Roxy,Md Rubel Ahmed*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SwiftCTS 是一款轻量级的物理启发式代理框架，能在无需重训练的情况下快速且精准地评估时钟树综合（CTS）的各项指标，极大地加速了物理设计空间的探索与优化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时钟树综合（CTS）流程计算开销巨大，且现有机器学习方法在处理未见过的架构时往往需要耗时的再训练或微调，难以满足大规模组合搜索对评估效率的需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SwiftCTS 的物理启发式代理框架。该框架利用轻量级的物理统计特征结合梯度提升决策树（Gradient-Boosted Ensembles）进行预测；引入了 K-shot 乘法校准机制，在无需重新训练的情况下实现对未知架构（OOD）的高精度适配；并将该引擎集成于进化优化器中以执行快速搜索。

Result: SwiftCTS 在 CPU 上训练时间低于 5 秒，推理时间在毫秒级以内；在未知架构上，将功率预测误差从 24.5% 降至 3.3%，线长误差从 56.6% 降至 1% 以下；通过进化算法在 10 秒内完成 10 万次配置评估，闭环验证显示功率和线长误差低于 0.5%，时序偏差预测精度在 5 皮秒以内。

Conclusion: SwiftCTS 通过物理启发式特征与高效机器学习模型的结合，成功解决了时钟树综合中计算成本高昂和对新设计架构适应性差的问题，为物理设计流程提供了一种高精度、极速的替代方案，展现了在自动化物理设计中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Clock Tree Synthesis (CTS) is a computationally expensive stage in the physical design flow, requiring iterative EDA tool invocations to navigate a vast configuration space for optimal power, wirelength, and timing skew. Existing machine learning approaches require computationally expensive retraining or fine-tuning cycles to adapt to unseen macro architectures and are architecturally mismatched to the millions of evaluations demanded by exhaustive combinatorial search. We present SwiftCTS, a physics-informed surrogate framework that addresses both limitations simultaneously. By coupling lightweight, physics-grounded statistical features with gradient-boosted ensembles, SwiftCTS trains in under five seconds on a CPU and delivers sub-millisecond inference without GPU support. To handle out-of-distribution (OOD) designs without retraining or fine-tuning, we introduce a K-shot multiplicative calibration mechanism that anchors predictions to just one or two physical reference runs, reducing power prediction error from 24.5\% to 3.3\% and wirelength error from 56.6\% to under 1\% on unseen macros. Integrating this engine with an evolutionary optimizer, SwiftCTS evaluates 100,000 CTS configurations in under ten seconds, yielding Pareto-optimal frontiers that are physically validated within the OpenROAD flow. Closed-loop validation confirms prediction errors below 0.5\% for power and wirelength, and timing skew predictions within five picoseconds on an OOD benchmark, consistently outperforming default tool heuristics across all target metrics. Code publicly available at: \href{https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SwiftCTS-7E6E}{https://github.com/BarsatKhadka/SwiftCTS}

</details>


### [112] [GLACIER: A Multimodal Student-Teacher Foundation Model for Molecular Property Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11382)
*Emily Nguyen,Yongchan Hong,Harsh Toshniwal,Yan Liu,Andreas Luttens*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着分子发现领域对模型规模需求的增长，计算负担日益沉重，且现有大规模模型多为单模态，未能充分利用分子数据的互补性。因此，该研究旨在通过多模态融合与知识蒸馏，开发一种既高效又具有高性能的分子表征学习框架。

Method: GLACIER 模型采用包含三个阶段的学生-教师框架：1. 针对分子图（图神经网络）、SMILES 序列（Transformer）和物理化学描述符（MLP）分别进行预训练；2. 利用创新的 Finsler 几何感知模块融合上述三种模态；3. 通过对比学习，将 MiniMol 和 MolFormer 等大型教师模型的知识蒸馏至轻量级学生模型中。

Result: 实验结果表明，GLACIER 框架在复杂的分子属性预测任务中表现出极高的预测性能，同时具备优异的计算效率，有效地平衡了模型性能与可扩展性。

Conclusion: GLACIER 通过结合多模态数据与知识蒸馏技术，成功在保持轻量化和高效性的同时，提升了分子属性预测任务的准确性，证明了跨模态对齐在分子表征学习中的有效性。

Abstract: Deep learning models facilitate the discovery of molecules with tailored properties among billions of candidate compounds. However, the computational burden to develop and deploy state-of-the-art models continuously increases, limiting their scalability. Most large-scale models are unimodal in nature and overlook the potential to leverage complementary molecular data modalities. To address these shortcomings, this paper introduces the Graph-Language Alignment for Chemical Inference and Exploration using Representations (GLACIER) model, a student-teacher framework that integrates molecular graphs, SMILES strings, and physicochemical descriptors to learn rich molecular embeddings. Our framework consists of three stages: (1) we pretrain three student encoders on 100,000 drug-like molecules: a message-passing neural network for molecular graphs, a transformer-based encoder for SMILES strings, and a multilayer perceptron for physicochemical descriptors, (2) we fuse these student modalities using a novel Finsler geometry-aware module, and (3) distill complementary knowledge from large teacher models, including MiniMol and MolFormer, into a single lightweight model via contrastive learning. We demonstrate that GLACIER is a robust framework that delivers high predictive performance and computational efficiency in complex molecular property prediction tasks. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/eemokey/glacier.
